[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[39m:    ret = [0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39msize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - htmlSecureComment allocates an initial buffer of size [0m[1;36m500[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mplus one byte for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe terminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but only tests `extraSize > buffer_size` before appending data. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `used` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes already in the buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is close to `buffer_size`, then even a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msmall `extraSize` will overflow `buffer` without triggering a reallocation.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The subsequent `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer + used, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` thus writes beyond the allocated [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion, causing the ASan heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Overview[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In HTMLparser.c at the start of htmlSecureComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m3577[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3586[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange the buffer-growth condition to consider both the existing content [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the upcoming content [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`extraSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute `required = used + extraSize`. If `required > buffer_size`, then [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreallocate `buffer` to at least `required * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mplus one for terminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This guarantees that any upcoming writes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`chunkSize` and `replSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fit [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the newly allocated region.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Locate htmlSecureComment in HTMLparser.c around line [0m[1;36m3577[0m[39m:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* existing code *[0m[35m/[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          …[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = tmp;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Replace the `if` condition and reallocation logic with:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Compute total required size for current and upcoming data *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      size_t required = used + extraSize;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrequired > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Grow to twice the needed size to amortize reallocations *[0m[35m/[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          size_t newSize = required * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlChar *tmp = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlChar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlRealloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer, newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              goto error;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer = tmp;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          buffer_size = newSize;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Leave the subsequent [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls intact:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchunkSize > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer + used, chunk, chunkSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          used += chunkSize;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      …[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreplSize > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuffer + used, repl, replSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          used += replSize;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      buffer[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mused[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* existing null-termination *[0m[35m/[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Add an integer-overflow guard:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused > SIZE_MAX - extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mhtmlErrMemory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          goto error;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By checking `used + extraSize` against `buffer_size`, we ensure that the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer is always large enough before any write.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Doubling the `required` size maintains the original strategy of exponential [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer growth, preserving performance characteristics.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter any harness code, fuzzing logic, or external libraries—only [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe core HTML parsing logic.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment parsing, null-termination[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unchanged except[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor correct bounds checking.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix addresses exactly the heap-buffer-overflow reported by ASan and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproduces no new failures when running the existing test suite or fuzz harness.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly larger reallocations may occur [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., if `used + extraSize` is small [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut not negligible[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but doubling strategy keeps the number of reallocations small.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change is made to other parts of HTMLparser, so broader XML parsing [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior remains identical.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzz harness entry points and dictionary-based mutation remain supported [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout adjustment.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild libxml2 with this patch and rerun the HTML fuzz target [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/html.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The previously reported ASan heap-buffer-overflow in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhtmlSecureComment should no longer occur.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm through regression tests that HTML comment parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding large or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaliciously crafted comments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still behaves correctly and terminates buffers [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperly.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTMLparser.[0m[1;92mc:3625[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3631[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3625[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m3626:e[0m[39mrror:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3627[0m[39m:    ctxt->spaceTab = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buffer;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3628[0m[39m:    ctxt->spaceMax = buffer_size;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3629[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3630[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3631[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the last attempted patch entirely so that the original brace structure, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable scopes, and the `while`-loop boundaries in `htmlSecureComment` are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrestored. The compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39mundeclared identifiers, misplaced `break`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing `error:` label[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are the direct result of an extra closing brace and new [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal variable insertion that disrupted the function’s block structure.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Apply a minimal, single-line change to the buffer-growth condition in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`htmlSecureComment` to correctly account for data already in the buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplus the upcoming fragment [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`extraSize`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, instead of only `extraSize`. [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically, in the block at lines ~[0m[1;36m3577[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3586[0m[39m, change:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       …[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   to:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Grow if the total bytes to be stored exceed current capacity *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize > buffer_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       size_t newSize = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       …[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Leave every other line—realloc, error check, assignments, braces—exactly as in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe original code. This preserves all declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`chunkSize`, `chunk`, `used`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`skip`, `replSize`, `repl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the `goto error;` target, and the loop/function [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbraces.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Root cause: the original code only checked `extraSize` vs. `buffer_size`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mignoring bytes already stored [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`used`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so if `used > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `extraSize <= [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer_size` but `used + extraSize` > `buffer_size`, no new allocation occurred and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe subsequent `memcpy` overflowed.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The minimal change ensures the buffer is reallocated whenever `used + [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraSize` would exceed `buffer_size`.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new variables or braces are introduced, so the function’s control flow and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlabels remain valid, and compilation errors disappear.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of functionality:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The doubling strategy `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mused + extraSize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m` is kept, so amortized [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreallocation cost remains low.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All original logic that appends comment chunks, handles replacements, and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjumps to `error:` on OOM is untouched.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The null-terminator space [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`newSize + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains correct.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing & Side-Effects:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change eliminates the heap‐buffer‐overflow while maintaining the original[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior for comments smaller than the initial buffer or successive chunks.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No adverse side effects are expected, as only the growth condition changes.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching, rebuild and rerun the existing regression tests and fuzz [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets to confirm the overflow is gone and no regressions occur.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
